headers nominated by the Connection header\\n  - Rejecting if Connection nominates x-forwarded-* headers or pseudo-headers (RFC violation)\\n  - Sanitizing the TE (Transfer-Encoding) header when path normalization with escaped slash handling\\n\\n### HTTP/2 Specific Validation  \\n\\n**HTTP/2 Forbidden Headers (source/extensions/http/header_validators/envoy_default/http2_header_validator.cc)**\\n- Enforces strict validation that connection-specific headers are forbidden in HTTP/2 per RFC 9113\\n- Forbidden header list: transfer-encoding, connection, upgrade, keep-alive, proxy-connection\\n- Returns ConnectionHeaderSanitization rejection code (uhv.http2.connection_header_rejected) when these headers are detected\\n- Validates header names are lowercase (HTTP/2 requirement)\\n- Rejects headers with uppercase letters (HTTP/2 compliance)\\n- Rejects header names with underscores if configured (headers_with_underscores_action)\\n- Validates empty header names are rejected\\n\\n### Path and Query Validation\\n\\n**Path Validation (source/extensions/http/header_validators/envoy_default/header_validator.cc)**\\n- `validatePathHeaderCharacters()`: Validates path contains only RFC 3986 compliant characters\\n- Normalizes paths and validates encoded sequences\\n- Supports disabling path normalization while still validating character sets\\n- Detects and prevents null byte injection (%00) in paths\\n- against HTTP/2 semantics (QUIC uses HTTP/2 header encoding)\\n\\n**QUIC Utilities (source/common/quic/envoy_quic_utils.h)**\\n- `quicHeadersToEnvoyHeaders()`: Converts QUIC headers to Envoy format with validation\\n- Enforces max header count and size limits during conversion\\n- Supports header validator interface for custom validation\\n\\n### Header Underscore Handling\\n\\n**Underscore Sanitization (source/extensions/http/header_validators/envoy_default/header_validator.cc)**\\n- `sanitizeHeadersWithUnderscores()`: Drops or rejects headers containing underscores\\n- Configurable via for path characters\\n\\n### Architecture Summary\\n\\nThe header injection prevention is enforced at multiple levels:\\n\\n1. **Codec Level**: HTTP/1, HTTP/2, and HTTP/3 codecs validate headers path normalization with escaped slash handling\\n\\n### HTTP/2 Specific Validation  \\n\\n**HTTP/2 Forbidden Headers (source/extensions/http/header_validators/envoy_default/http2_header_validator.cc)**\\n- Enforces strict validation that connection-specific headers are forbidden in HTTP/2 per RFC 9113\\n- Forbidden header list: transfer-encoding, connection, upgrade, keep-alive, proxy-connection\\n- Returns ConnectionHeaderSanitization rejection code (uhv.http2.connection_header_rejected) when these headers are detected\\n- Validates header names are lowercase (HTTP/2 requirement)\\n- Rejects headers with uppercase letters (HTTP/2 compliance)\\n- Rejects header names with underscores if configured
